 tippaniyan Sea Harrier in Goa will be given a traditional farewell in the presence of Naval Chief Admiral Robin Dhawan
 33 saal kii seva ke baad ye ritair ho rahaa he
 The Indian Navy bought these fighter jets from Britain in 1983
 nausena main aane ke baad ye pehle vimaan vaahak pot vikrant or uske baad phir viraat main tainaat ho gaye

 chaar ank lekar bharat behatar net ranret ke aadhaar par talika main duusare sthaan par he
 Bangladesh also have four points but are in third place
 tippaniyan Now India will have to depend on the outcome of the last league match to be played between Bangladesh and Sri Lanka to reach the final
 yah match yadi bangladesh jeet jaati he to bangladesh kaa final kaa tikat tay ho jayega
 The Sri Lankan team has been eliminated from the competition
 kohli ne apane kariyar kaa 11waan shatak shandaar andaaj main puraa kiya
 Kohli scored 183 runs in 148 balls with the help of 22 fours and a six
 kohli ne pehle sachin tendulkar ke saath 133 or phir rohit sharma ke saath 172 ranon kii pari kheli
 Kohli was dismissed in the 48th over
 bharat kii ore se gautam gambheer or sachin tendulkar ne pari kii shuruyaat kii
 Mohammad Hafeez dismissed Gambhir lbw on the second ball of the first over
 is samay bharat kaa khaataa bhi nahin khulaa tha
 India's second wicket fell as Sachin Tendulkar
 sachin ne kohli ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 133 ran jode
 Sachin hit five fours and a six in his 52-ball innings
 rohit sharma ne 83 gendon main paanch chauke or ek chakke kii madad se 68 ran banaae
 He was dismissed in the 46th over
 suresh raina 12 or mahendra singh dhoni chaar ran banaakar naabad rahe
 For Pakistan, Umar Gul got two successes, while Mohammad Hafeez and Saeed Ajmal got one wicket each
 isse pehle, toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karne utari pakistani team ne nirdhaarit 50 overon kii samaapti tak chah wicket par 329 ran banaae
 For him, opener Mohammad Hafeez scored 105, Nasir Jamshed 112 and former captain Younis Khan scored 52 runs
 hafeez ne kariyar kaa chauthaa or nasir ne pehla shatak lagaaya
 Umar Akmal also added 28 runs
 nasir or hafeez ne pehle wicket ke liye 224 ran jodakar apni team ko majboot aadhaar diya
 For India, Praveen Kumar and Ashok Dinda got two wickets, while Ravichandran Ashwin and Irfan Pathan got one success each
 pakistan kii shuruyaat joardaar rahi
 Hafeez teamed up with Nasir to score his maiden century against India
 5 overon main 224 ran jode
 Pakistani players gave the Indian bowlers a wicket for wickets on the basis of excellent batting
 hafeez sabase pehle 103 gendon par apana chauthaa shatak puraa kiya
 Hafeez kissed the pitch after completing a century
 iske baad nasir ne shatak puraa kiya
 Nasir faced 98 balls for this
 nasir 224 ran ke kul yoga par sabase pehle pavilion laute
 After this, Dinda also walked Hafeez for a total of 225 runs
 iske baad umr akmal or younis khan ne tisare wicket ke liye 38 ran jode
 Umar was dismissed for a total of 273 runs
 umr kii vidaai ke baad shahid afridi (9) or hamad ajam (4) kuch khaas nahin kar sake or kramash: pathan tathaa dinda kaa shikaar bane
 Meanwhile, Younis completed his half-century
 vah praveen kii gend par behtareen tareeke se suresh raina ke haathon lapke gaye
 Captain Misbal ul Haq returned unbeaten on four runs

 bharat kaa doosraa wicket sachin tendulkar ke rup main gira
 Sachin along with Kohli added 133 runs for the second wicket
 sachin ne apni 52 gendon kii pari main paanch chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Rohit Sharma scored 68 runs in 83 balls with the help of five fours and a six
 vah 46wein over main out hue
 Suresh Raina 12 and Mahendra Singh Dhoni remained unbeaten with four runs
 pakistan kii ore se umr gul ko do safalataa mili jabaki mohammad hafeez or said ajmal ko ek-ek wicket mila
 Earlier, after winning the toss, the Pakistani team came out to bat first and scored 329 for six wickets till the end of the scheduled 50 overs
 uske liye salaami ballebaaj mohammad hafeez ne 105, nasir jamshed ne 112 or purv captain younis khan ne 52 ranon kii pari kheli
 Hafeez scored his fourth career and Nasir scored his first century
 umr akmal ne bhi 28 ran jode
 Nasir and Hafeez added 224 runs for the first wicket to give their team a strong base
 bharat kii ore se praveen kumaar or ashok dinda ko do wicket mili jabaki ravichandran aswin or irfan pathan ko ek-ek safalataa mili
 Pakistan started strongly
 bharat ke khilaaf apana pehla shatak lagane vaale hafeez ne nasir ke saath milakar 35
 224 runs in 5 overs
 pakistani khilaadiyon ne shandaar ballebaaji ke dam par bhartiya gendbaajon ko wicket ke liye tarasaa diya
 Hafeez first completed his fourth century off 103 balls
 shatak puraa karne ke baad hafeez ne pich ko choomaa
 Nasir then completed a century
 nasir ne iske liye 98 gendon kaa saamana kiya
 Nasir returned to the pavilion for the first time with a total of 224 runs
 iske baad 225 ran ke kul yoga par dinda ne hafeez ko bhi chalata kiya
 After this, Umar Akmal and Younis Khan added 38 runs for the third wicket
 umr 273 ranon ke kul yoga par out hue
 After Omar's departure, Shahid Afridi (9) and Hamad Azam (4) could not do anything special and became victims of Pathan and Dinda respectively
 isi bich younis ne apana ardhashatak puraa kiya
 He was caught in the hands of Suresh Raina at the ball of Praveen
 captain misbal ul haq chaar ran par naabad laute
 The Pakistani team has now won both their matches played
 nau ankon ke saath pakistan talika main sheersh par he jabaki bhartiya team bhi itane hi match khel chuki he jinamein se use ek main jeet jabaki ek match main haar mili he
 India are at the second place in the table based on better net runs by four points
 bangladesh ke bhi chaar ank he lekin vah tisare sthaan par he
 The comments ab bharat ko final main pahunchane ke liye use bangladesh or srilanka ke bich khele jane vaale aakhri lig mukaable ke nattejey par nirbhar rahanaa padegaa

 srilankai team pratiyogita se baahar ho chuki he
 Of the 192 iron mines in Odisha, 94 are operating illegally
 rajya main ho rahi aayran mining kii jaanch ke liye bane shah kamishan kii report main yah khulaasa hua he
 This report is yet to be presented in Parliament, but according to information received by NDTV, 94 mines out of 192 have no environmental clearance
 jin 96 khadaanon ke paas kanoonee rup se anumati he, ve apni seemaa se adhik loha nikaal rahe hai
 There are 56 mines which are in the forest protected area, where mining cannot be done without the permission of the Forest Department
 justise shah kii report main gaiyrkanoonee khanan ke liye centre or rajya donon sarkarein jimmedaar hai
